React, { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\nimport ace from 'ace-builds';\nimport 'ace-builds/src-noconflict/mode-lua';\nimport 'ace-builds/src-noconflict/theme-monokai';\nimport 'ace-builds/src-noconflict/ext-language_tools';\n// Import the necessary extension for virtual scrolling if needed,\n// though Ace often handles it well by default.\n// No specific import usually required just for virtual scrolling itself.\n\ninterface CodeEditorProps {\n  initialValue: string;\n  onChange: (value: string) => void;\n}\n\nconst CodeEditor: React.FC<CodeEditorProps> = ({ initialValue, onChange }) => {\n  const editorRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const aceEditorRef = useRef<ace.Ace.Editor | null>(null); // Use Ace types\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!editorRef.current) return;\n\n    // Initialize Ace Editor\n    aceEditorRef.current = ace.edit(editorRef.current);\n    const editor = aceEditorRef.current;\n\n    // --- MODIFIED OPTIONS ---\n    editor.setOptions({\n      // Theme and Mode\n      theme: 'ace/theme/monokai',\n      mode: 'ace/mode/lua',\n\n      // Basic Functionality\n      enableBasicAutocompletion: true,\n      enableLiveAutocompletion: true,\n      enableSnippets: true,\n      showLineNumbers: true,\n      tabSize: 2,\n      useWorker: true, // Use web workers for performance (good practice)\n\n      // Appearance & Behavior\n      fontSize: 14,\n      showGutter: true, // Keep line numbers visible\n      highlightActiveLine: true,\n      highlightSelectedWord: true,\n\n      // --- NEW/MODIFIED OPTIONS ---\n      // Virtual Scrolling (Ace handles this largely automatically,\n      // maxLines ensures it can handle large files efficiently)\n      maxLines: Infinity,\n\n      // Disable Minimap (Ace doesn't have a built-in minimap like Monaco.\n      // This often refers to disabling the print margin line)\n      showPrintMargin: false,\n\n      // Disable Auto Scroll beyond the last line\n      scrollPastEnd: false,\n      // --- END NEW/MODIFIED OPTIONS ---\n    });\n    // --- END MODIFIED OPTIONS ---\n\n    // Set initial value without moving cursor/scrolling to the end\n    // The second argument (-1) places the cursor at the beginning (row 0, col 0)\n    editor.setValue(initialValue, -1);\n\n    // Add change listener\n    const changeListener = () => {\n      if (aceEditorRef.current) {\n        const value = aceEditorRef.current.getValue();\n        onChange(value);\n      }\n    };\n    editor.on('change', changeListener);\n\n    // Ensure the editor resizes if the container resizes\n    // (Important for responsive layouts like ResizablePanelGroup)\n    const resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(() => {\n      editor.resize();\n    });\n    resizeObserver.observe(editorRef.current);\n\n\n    // Clean up\n    return () => {\n      resizeObserver.disconnect();\n      if (editor) {\n        // It's good practice to remove listeners you added\n        editor.off('change', changeListener);\n        editor.destroy();\n        // Optional: Explicitly release the reference from the container\n        const editorNode = editor.container;\n        if (editorNode) {\n            // @ts-ignore - Ace adds properties directly to the DOM element\n            delete editorNode.env;\n             // @ts-ignore\n            delete editorNode.renderer;\n             // @ts-ignore\n            delete editorNode.session;\n             // @ts-ignore\n            delete editorNode.$mouseHandler;\n        }\n\n      }\n      aceEditorRef.current = null;\n    };\n    // Only run effect when initialValue or onChange changes.\n    // Avoid re-initializing the editor unnecessarily.\n  }, [onChange]); // Removed initialValue from dependency array\n\n  // Handle external changes to initialValue if necessary\n  // This prevents re-initializing the whole editor when the prop changes,\n  // which would lose editor state (like cursor position, undo history).\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (aceEditorRef.current && aceEditorRef.current.getValue() !== initialValue) {\n      const cursorPosition = aceEditorRef.current.getCursorPosition();\n      aceEditorRef.current.setValue(initialValue, -1); // Set value, move cursor to start\n      // Optionally restore cursor if needed, but often resetting is fine\n      // aceEditorRef.current.moveCursorToPosition(cursorPosition);\n      // aceEditorRef.current.clearSelection(); // Clear selection after setting value\n    }\n  }, [initialValue]);\n\n\n
